<hr data-start="3518" data-end="3521">
<h3 data-section-id="jvhpma" data-start="3523" data-end="3551">✅ Features in this code:</h3>
<ol data-start="3552" data-end="3806">
<li data-section-id="nm8mk8" data-start="3552" data-end="3587">
<p data-start="3555" data-end="3587"><strong data-start="3555" data-end="3569">Dark theme</strong> with modern UI.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1np5bal" data-start="3588" data-end="3625">
<p data-start="3591" data-end="3625">Input for <strong data-start="3601" data-end="3622">video description</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1cj5rlr" data-start="3626" data-end="3684">
<p data-start="3629" data-end="3684">A <strong data-start="3631" data-end="3650">generate button</strong> that triggers video generation.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="19l4rw6" data-start="3685" data-end="3724">
<p data-start="3688" data-end="3724">Video player embedded on the page.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="di4b1k" data-start="3725" data-end="3806">
<p data-start="3728" data-end="3806">Fully responsive and GitHub-ready (just push to repo and open <code data-start="3790" data-end="3802">index.html</code>).</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="3808" data-end="3811">
<h3 data-section-id="u880cd" data-start="3813" data-end="3861">🔹 How to make it a real AI video generator:</h3>
<ul data-start="3862" data-end="4093">
<li data-section-id="31kr6r" data-start="3862" data-end="3973">
<p data-start="3864" data-end="3973">Replace the placeholder video URL with an actual <strong data-start="3913" data-end="3934">AI video API call</strong> (e.g., <strong data-start="3942" data-end="3969">Runway, Sora, Pika Labs</strong>).</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="oybmid" data-start="3974" data-end="4043">
<p data-start="3976" data-end="4043">Use <code data-start="3980" data-end="3989">fetch()</code> to send <code data-start="3998" data-end="4004">text</code> to the API and get back a video URL.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1dim66j" data-start="4044" data-end="4093">
<p data-start="4046" data-end="4093">Assign the returned URL to <code data-start="4073" data-end="4090">videoPlayer.src</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="4095" data-end="4098">
<p data-start="4100" data-end="4160">If you want, I can make an <strong data-start="4127" data-end="4157">even more advanced version</strong>:</p>
<ul data-start="4161" data-end="4303">
<li data-section-id="1vwlxna" data-start="4161" data-end="4194">
<p data-start="4163" data-end="4194"><strong data-start="4163" data-end="4192">Drag &amp; drop video uploads</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="zqgxus" data-start="4195" data-end="4234">
<p data-start="4197" data-end="4234"><strong data-start="4197" data-end="4232">Custom AI video API integration</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="dvvpgw" data-start="4235" data-end="4266">
<p data-start="4237" data-end="4266"><strong data-start="4237" data-end="4264">Multiple video previews</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ixr78w" data-start="4267" data-end="4303">
<p data-start="4269" data-end="4303"><strong data-start="4269" data-end="4301">Better dark theme animations</strong></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="4305" data-end="4360">This would still be <strong data-start="4325" data-end="4357">single-page and GitHub-ready</strong>.</p>

<h2 data-section-id="ad61jc" data-start="189" data-end="225"><span role="text"><strong data-start="192" data-end="225">Step 1: GitHub Account Banaye</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="226" data-end="329">
<li data-section-id="5r047q" data-start="226" data-end="302">
<p data-start="229" data-end="302">Agar account nahi hai, to <a data-start="255" data-end="284" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="decorated-link" href="https://github.com/">GitHub<span aria-hidden="true" class="ms-0.5 inline-block align-middle leading-none"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" data-rtl-flip="" class="block h-[0.75em] w-[0.75em] stroke-current stroke-[0.75]"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#304883" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></span></a> pe signup karein.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="16zegk5" data-start="303" data-end="329">
<p data-start="306" data-end="329">Free plan hi kaafi hai.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="331" data-end="334">
<h2 data-section-id="1hw7dsh" data-start="336" data-end="372"><span role="text"><strong data-start="339" data-end="372">Step 2: New Repository Banaye</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="373" data-end="647">
<li data-section-id="1omn27j" data-start="373" data-end="432">
<p data-start="376" data-end="432">GitHub me login karein → <strong data-start="401" data-end="417">Repositories</strong> tab → <strong data-start="424" data-end="431">New</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="iifibg" data-start="433" data-end="491">
<p data-start="436" data-end="491">Repository ka naam: <code data-start="456" data-end="473">video-generator</code> (ya jo chahen).</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="195ciec" data-start="492" data-end="519">
<p data-start="495" data-end="519">Description: Optional.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="17gy7ky" data-start="520" data-end="550">
<p data-start="523" data-end="550"><strong data-start="523" data-end="533">Public</strong> select karein.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="8xm2tt" data-start="551" data-end="601">
<p data-start="554" data-end="601">Checkbox <strong data-start="563" data-end="586">“Add a README file”</strong> tick karein.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1eissyf" data-start="602" data-end="647">
<p data-start="605" data-end="647"><strong data-start="605" data-end="626">Create repository</strong> button click karein.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="649" data-end="652">
<h2 data-section-id="slyhj3" data-start="654" data-end="701"><span role="text"><strong data-start="657" data-end="701">Step 3: Apni Website Files Upload Karein</strong></span></h2>
<p data-start="702" data-end="806">Aapke paas <code data-start="713" data-end="725">index.html</code> file ready honi chahiye (maine pehle aapko dark video generator ka code diya).</p>
<h3 data-section-id="16fuma7" data-start="808" data-end="844">Option 1: Direct Upload (Simple)</h3>
<ol data-start="845" data-end="989">
<li data-section-id="1iis7zk" data-start="845" data-end="905">
<p data-start="848" data-end="905">Repository me jaayein → <strong data-start="872" data-end="884">Add file</strong> → <strong data-start="887" data-end="903">Upload files</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="zvmu9n" data-start="906" data-end="946">
<p data-start="909" data-end="946"><code data-start="909" data-end="921">index.html</code> ko drag &amp; drop karein.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1j2tpsg" data-start="947" data-end="989">
<p data-start="950" data-end="989"><strong data-start="950" data-end="968">Commit changes</strong> button click karein.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 data-section-id="103wh8h" data-start="991" data-end="1032">Option 2: Git Command Line (Advanced)</h3>
<p data-start="1033" data-end="1068">Agar aap Git install kiye hue hain:</p>

<h2 data-section-id="gjkptz" data-start="1266" data-end="1307"><span role="text"><strong data-start="1269" data-end="1307">Step 4: GitHub Pages Enable Karein</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="1308" data-end="1555">
<li data-section-id="1oorjzp" data-start="1308" data-end="1355">
<p data-start="1311" data-end="1355">Repository me <strong data-start="1325" data-end="1337">Settings</strong> tab me jaayein.</p>

<li data-section-id="1ju1s7w" data-start="1356" data-end="1401">

</li>
<li data-section-id="ejncl0" data-start="1402" data-end="1524">
<p data-start="1405" data-end="1421"><strong data-start="1405" data-end="1415">Source</strong> me:</p>
<ul data-start="1425" data-end="1524">
<li data-section-id="odma3s" data-start="1425" data-end="1457">
<p data-start="1427" data-end="1457">Branch: <code data-start="1435" data-end="1441">main</code> (ya <code data-start="1446" data-end="1454">master</code>)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1886ki3" data-start="1461" data-end="1524">
<p data-start="1463" data-end="1524">Folder: <code data-start="1471" data-end="1478">/root</code> (ya <code data-start="1483" data-end="1490">/docs</code> agar files docs folder me hain)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1oe7bip" data-start="1525" data-end="1555">
<p data-start="1528" data-end="1555"><strong data-start="1528" data-end="1536">Save</strong> pe click karein.</p>
</li>
</ol>

<h3 data-section-id="1bjwpxi" data-start="1879" data-end="1891">🔹 Tips:</h3>
<ul data-start="1892" data-end="2171">
<li data-section-id="35bghy" data-start="1892" data-end="2000">
<p data-start="1894" data-end="2000">Agar aap <strong data-start="1903" data-end="1935">CSS aur JS ko separate files</strong> me daalte hain, ensure karein ki <code data-start="1969" data-end="1981">index.html</code> me sahi path ho.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="hhxrp1" data-start="2001" data-end="2087">
<p data-start="2003" data-end="2087">Har update ke baad <strong data-start="2022" data-end="2039">commit &amp; push</strong> karein, GitHub automatically update kar dega.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="j8i515" data-start="2088" data-end="2171">
<p data-start="2090" data-end="2171">Free plan me ye <strong data-start="2106" data-end="2115">HTTPS</strong> link bhi support karta hai, koi hosting charges nahi.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<p data-start="2178" data-end="2376">Agar chaho to main aapke liye <strong data-start="2208" data-end="2251">ready-to-upload GitHub folder structure</strong> bana doon jisme <code data-start="2268" data-end="2280">index.html</code>, <code data-start="2282" data-end="2293">style.css</code>, aur <code data-start="2299" data-end="2310">script.js</code> alag files me ho aur turant <strong data-start="2339" data-end="2373">GitHub Pages pe deploy ho jaye</strong>.</p>

<h1 data-section-id="be250z" data-start="390" data-end="480"><span role="text"><strong data-start="392" data-end="480">Step by Step: GitHub pe Single-Page Website Deploy karna (Dark Video Generator Tool)</strong></span></h1>

<h2 data-section-id="1hw7dsh" data-start="601" data-end="637"><span role="text"><strong data-start="604" data-end="637">Step 2: New Repository Banaye</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="638" data-end="986">
<li data-section-id="ek7d2" data-start="638" data-end="708">
<p data-start="641" data-end="708">GitHub homepage pe <strong data-start="660" data-end="665">+</strong> icon → <strong data-start="673" data-end="691">New repository</strong> select karein.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1tvuzbm" data-start="709" data-end="764">
<p data-start="712" data-end="764">Repository name: <code data-start="729" data-end="746">video-generator</code> (ya jo chahen).</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="195ciec" data-start="765" data-end="792">
<p data-start="768" data-end="792">Description: Optional.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1qpe14z" data-start="793" data-end="853">
<p data-start="796" data-end="853"><strong data-start="796" data-end="806">Public</strong> select karein (taake website accessible ho).</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="14teamo" data-start="854" data-end="938">
<p data-start="857" data-end="938"><strong data-start="857" data-end="878">Do not initialize</strong> with README, .gitignore, ya license (later optional hai).</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="14s5fdj" data-start="939" data-end="986">
<p data-start="942" data-end="986"><strong data-start="942" data-end="963">Create repository</strong> button click karein.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote data-start="988" data-end="1034">
<p data-start="990" data-end="1034">Ab aapke paas ek khali repository ready hai.</p>
</blockquote>

<p data-start="4250" data-end="4294">Is file ko <code data-start="4261" data-end="4273">index.html</code> naam se save karein.</p>

<h2 data-section-id="lj2tio" data-start="4301" data-end="4338"><span role="text"><strong data-start="4304" data-end="4338">Step 5: Upload Files to GitHub</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="4339" data-end="4482">
<li data-section-id="1iis7zk" data-start="4339" data-end="4399">
<p data-start="4342" data-end="4399">Repository me jaayein → <strong data-start="4366" data-end="4378">Add file</strong> → <strong data-start="4381" data-end="4397">Upload files</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="dopzgf" data-start="4400" data-end="4437">

<li data-section-id="uduv2o" data-start="4438" data-end="4482">

<p data-start="4486" data-end="4528">Ab aapki website GitHub repository me hai.</p>

<h3 data-section-id="1iogngk" data-start="5818" data-end="5836"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="5824" data-end="5836">Features</strong></span></h3>
<ol data-start="5837" data-end="6082">
<li data-section-id="3fphiz" data-start="5837" data-end="5867">
<p data-start="5840" data-end="5867">Dark theme, GitHub ready.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1d2rb0v" data-start="5868" data-end="5913">
<p data-start="5871" data-end="5913">Tabs: <strong data-start="5877" data-end="5910">Text / Image / Voice to video</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="9kp1ic" data-start="5914" data-end="5967">
<p data-start="5917" data-end="5967">Video <strong data-start="5923" data-end="5935">duration</strong> and <strong data-start="5940" data-end="5956">aspect ratio</strong> control.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="8qwy9l" data-start="5968" data-end="6039">
<p data-start="5971" data-end="6039">Placeholder video, ready to integrate with <strong data-start="6014" data-end="6036">Sora/Pika Labs API</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="19uayl8" data-start="6040" data-end="6082">
<p data-start="6043" data-end="6082">Fully single-page, responsive design.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="6084" data-end="6087">
<p data-start="6089" data-end="6205">Agar chaho, main ab <strong data-start="6109" data-end="6122">next step</strong> me aapke liye <strong data-start="6137" data-end="6185">actual AI video API integration wala version</strong> bana doon, jisme:</p>
<ul data-start="6207" data-end="6347">
<li data-section-id="1wjyllj" data-start="6207" data-end="6228">
<p data-start="6209" data-end="6228"><strong data-start="6209" data-end="6226">Text -&gt; Video</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="xuq63x" data-start="6229" data-end="6251">
<p data-start="6231" data-end="6251"><strong data-start="6231" data-end="6249">Image -&gt; Video</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ggodzw" data-start="6252" data-end="6274">
<p data-start="6254" data-end="6274"><strong data-start="6254" data-end="6272">Voice -&gt; Video</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1fukvme" data-start="6275" data-end="6313">
<p data-start="6277" data-end="6313">Ratio &amp; duration automatically set</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="rupsc6" data-start="6314" data-end="6347">
<p data-start="6316" data-end="6347">Direct download option bhi ho</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 data-section-id="1x983i6" data-start="5084" data-end="5104"><span role="text"><strong data-start="5088" data-end="5104">Step 1: Save</strong></span></h3>
<ol data-start="5105" data-end="5252">
<li data-section-id="hdp4zn" data-start="5105" data-end="5126">
<p data-start="5108" data-end="5126">Copy above code.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="fkapi2" data-start="5127" data-end="5173">
<p data-start="5130" data-end="5173">Open <strong data-start="5135" data-end="5170">Notepad / VSCode / Sublime Text</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1o7h86g" data-start="5174" data-end="5190">
<p data-start="5177" data-end="5190">Paste code.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="up7nfc" data-start="5191" data-end="5252">
<p data-start="5194" data-end="5252">Save as <strong data-start="5202" data-end="5218"><code data-start="5204" data-end="5216">index.html</code></strong> (important: extension <code data-start="5241" data-end="5248">.html</code>).</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="5254" data-end="5257">
<h3 data-section-id="1u72g4h" data-start="5259" data-end="5291"><span role="text"><strong data-start="5263" data-end="5291">Step 2: Upload to GitHub</strong></span></h3>
<ol data-start="5292" data-end="5450">
<li data-section-id="85s8mf" data-start="5292" data-end="5333">
<p data-start="5295" data-end="5333">Login GitHub → Open your repository.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1lzetju" data-start="5334" data-end="5373">
<p data-start="5337" data-end="5373">Click <strong data-start="5343" data-end="5370">Add file → Upload files</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1gfd8ol" data-start="5374" data-end="5411">
<p data-start="5377" data-end="5411">Drag &amp; drop your <strong data-start="5394" data-end="5408">index.html</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="2kv4ns" data-start="5412" data-end="5450">
<p data-start="5415" data-end="5450">Scroll down → <strong data-start="5429" data-end="5447">Commit changes</strong>.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="5452" data-end="5455">
<h3 data-section-id="4tt0pl" data-start="5457" data-end="5492"><span role="text"><strong data-start="5461" data-end="5492">Step 3: Enable GitHub Pages</strong></span></h3>
<ol data-start="5493" data-end="5622">
<li data-section-id="y238d" data-start="5493" data-end="5531">
<p data-start="5496" data-end="5531">Repository → <strong data-start="5509" data-end="5529">Settings → Pages</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="54ar4o" data-start="5532" data-end="5576">
<p data-start="5535" data-end="5576">Branch: <code data-start="5543" data-end="5549">main</code> → Folder: <code data-start="5560" data-end="5567">/root</code> → Save</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1howhvp" data-start="5577" data-end="5622">
<p data-start="5580" data-end="5622">GitHub URL milega → Open → Website live!</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="5624" data-end="5627">
<p data-start="5629" data-end="5710">✅ <strong data-start="5631" data-end="5707">Ab aapke paas ek single-file, dark theme, Sora-style interface ready hai</strong>.</p>
<p data-start="5712" data-end="5815">Agar chaho, main <strong data-start="5729" data-end="5805">ye version next step me actual AI video API connect karne wala bana doon</strong>, jisme:</p>
<ul data-start="5816" data-end="5938">
<li data-section-id="1jc8xxy" data-start="5816" data-end="5832">
<p data-start="5818" data-end="5832">Text → Video</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="xgju0c" data-start="5833" data-end="5850">
<p data-start="5835" data-end="5850">Image → Video</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="den4hp" data-start="5851" data-end="5868">
<p data-start="5853" data-end="5868">Voice → Video</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="vx66qv" data-start="5869" data-end="5905">
<p data-start="5871" data-end="5905">Duration &amp; ratio fully work kare</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1eq2fz7" data-start="5906" data-end="5938">
<p data-start="5908" data-end="5938">Direct video download option</p>
</li>

<h1 data-section-id="1tu2dap" data-start="150" data-end="191"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="154" data-end="191">Ab kya karna hai (IMPORTANT STEP)</strong></span></h1>
<h2 data-section-id="1l0p0i7" data-start="193" data-end="228"><span role="text"><strong data-start="196" data-end="228">Step 1: GitHub Pages ON karo</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="229" data-end="360">
<li data-section-id="1vlve25" data-start="229" data-end="259">
<p data-start="232" data-end="259">Apni repository open karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="vh8mzu" data-start="260" data-end="304">
<p data-start="263" data-end="304">Upar tabs me <strong data-start="276" data-end="288">Settings</strong> pe click karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="15x82xg" data-start="305" data-end="360">
<p data-start="308" data-end="360">Left side me scroll karo → <strong data-start="335" data-end="344">Pages</strong> pe click karo</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="362" data-end="365">
<h2 data-section-id="1pnbfi5" data-start="367" data-end="400"><span role="text"><strong data-start="370" data-end="400">Step 2: Source select karo</strong></span></h2>
<p data-start="401" data-end="435">Pages section me ye settings karo:</p>
<ul data-start="437" data-end="522">
<li data-section-id="1e8xnrj" data-start="437" data-end="474">
<p data-start="439" data-end="474"><strong data-start="439" data-end="449">Source</strong> → <code data-start="452" data-end="474">Deploy from a branch</code></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="tvba5h" data-start="475" data-end="496">
<p data-start="477" data-end="496"><strong data-start="477" data-end="487">Branch</strong> → <code data-start="490" data-end="496">main</code></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1qzujfo" data-start="497" data-end="522">
<p data-start="499" data-end="522"><strong data-start="499" data-end="509">Folder</strong> → <code data-start="512" data-end="522">/ (root)</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="524" data-end="551">Phir <strong data-start="529" data-end="537">Save</strong> pe click karo</p>
<hr data-start="553" data-end="556">
<h2 data-section-id="tt5tnh" data-start="558" data-end="595"><span role="text"><strong data-start="561" data-end="595">Step 3: Wait karo (1–2 minute)</strong></span></h2>
<p data-start="596" data-end="638">GitHub thoda time leta hai site banane me.</p>
<p data-start="640" data-end="674">Uske baad wahan ek link show hoga:</p>

<h2 data-section-id="ggu741" data-start="739" data-end="771"><span role="text"><strong data-start="742" data-end="771">Step 4: Website open karo</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="772" data-end="835">
<li data-section-id="4drro0" data-start="772" data-end="798">

<ul data-start="920" data-end="1026">
<li data-section-id="1bq1s2m" data-start="920" data-end="970">
<p data-start="922" data-end="970">File ka naam <strong data-start="935" data-end="970">exact <code data-start="943" data-end="955">index.html</code> hona chahiye</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="yktm2v" data-start="971" data-end="1026">
<p data-start="973" data-end="1026"><code data-start="973" data-end="989">index.html.txt</code> ya <code data-start="993" data-end="1008">index(1).html</code> nahi hona chahiye</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1028" data-end="1031">

</li>
</ul>

<h3 data-section-id="1udfu6n" data-start="1217" data-end="1240">✔️ Check 3: Refresh</h3>
<ul data-start="1241" data-end="1306">

<h1 data-section-id="jf4i18" data-start="1313" data-end="1340">🔥 Shortcut (Quick check)</h1>
<p data-start="1341" data-end="1356">Agar aap mujhe:</p>
<ul data-start="1357" data-end="1395">
<li data-section-id="1jmkef9" data-start="1357" data-end="1381">
<p data-start="1359" data-end="1381">apna GitHub username</p>
</li>

</li>

<p data-start="1397" data-end="1460">bata do, to main aapka <strong data-start="1420" data-end="1456">exact live link bana ke de dunga</strong> ✅</p>

<p data-start="1467" data-end="1507">Agar next level jaana hai to main aapko:</p>

<h1 data-section-id="1vbrwz8" data-start="141" data-end="180"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="145" data-end="180">Repository kahan se open karein</strong></span></h1>
<h2 data-section-id="7zlqua" data-start="182" data-end="211"><span role="text"><strong data-start="185" data-end="211">Method 1 (Sab se easy)</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="213" data-end="520">
<li data-section-id="g4k3d1" data-start="213" data-end="257">
<p data-start="216" data-end="257">Browser me jao:<br data-start="231" data-end="234">
👉 <a data-start="237" data-end="255" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="decorated-link" href="https://github.com/">https://github.com<span aria-hidden="true" class="ms-0.5 inline-block align-middle leading-none"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" data-rtl-flip="" class="block h-[0.75em] w-[0.75em] stroke-current stroke-[0.75]"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#304883" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></span></a></p>

<h1 data-section-id="1mbidlx" data-start="93" data-end="128"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="97" data-end="128">Best tareeka (Home Page se)</strong></span></h1>
<ol data-start="130" data-end="338">
<li data-section-id="mbbryt" data-start="130" data-end="176">
<p data-start="133" data-end="176"><strong data-start="133" data-end="153">GitHub open karo</strong> → <a data-start="156" data-end="174" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="decorated-link" href="https://github.com/">https://github.com<span aria-hidden="true" class="ms-0.5 inline-block align-middle leading-none"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" data-rtl-flip="" class="block h-[0.75em] w-[0.75em] stroke-current stroke-[0.75]"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#304883" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></span></a></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1udd4bx" data-start="177" data-end="192">
<p data-start="180" data-end="192">Login karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="xujwtz" data-start="193" data-end="241">
<p data-start="196" data-end="241">Top right me <strong data-start="209" data-end="225">profile icon</strong> pe click karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="19z72au" data-start="242" data-end="284">
<p data-start="245" data-end="284">Click karo 👉 <strong data-start="259" data-end="282">“Your repositories”</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="120wr0g" data-start="285" data-end="338">
<p data-start="288" data-end="338">Apni repo (e.g. <code data-start="304" data-end="321">video-generator</code>) pe click karo</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="340" data-end="389">👉 ✅ <strong data-start="345" data-end="389">Yahan se aapki repository open ho jayegi</strong></p>

<h1 data-section-id="6hugkq" data-start="396" data-end="439"><span role="text">🔹 <strong data-start="401" data-end="439">Navigation menu se bhi ja sakte ho</strong></span></h1>
<p data-start="441" data-end="477">Agar aap already GitHub ke andar ho:</p>
<ol data-start="479" data-end="612">

<p data-start="482" data-end="563">Top left me ya upar menu me <strong data-start="510" data-end="527">☰ (menu icon)</strong> ya <strong data-start="531" data-end="547">Repositories</strong> option milega</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="3geo4z" data-start="564" data-end="585">
<p data-start="567" data-end="585">Us pe click karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1na93t" data-start="586" data-end="612">
<p data-start="589" data-end="612">Apni repo select karo</p>
</li>
</ol>

<h1 data-section-id="iu4n26" data-start="619" data-end="641">🎯 Simple samajh lo:</h1>
<ul data-start="642" data-end="774">
<li data-section-id="19sp1m4" data-start="642" data-end="707">
<p data-start="644" data-end="707">Agar confuse ho → <strong data-start="662" data-end="705">Home page method use karo (recommended)</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="10z4ntc" data-start="708" data-end="774">

<h1 data-section-id="z3tl1n" data-start="198" data-end="244"><span role="text">🚨 <strong data-start="203" data-end="244">Sabse pehle ye check karo (IMPORTANT)</strong></span></h1>
<h2 data-section-id="8xo9pt" data-start="246" data-end="294"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="251" data-end="294">Step 1: Repo OPEN karo (sirf list nahi)</strong></span></h2>
<p data-start="295" data-end="336">Aap abhi shayad sirf list dekh rahe ho.</p>
<p data-start="338" data-end="362">👉 Aapko ye karna hai:</p>
<ul data-start="363" data-end="458">
<li data-section-id="1mkkn9s" data-start="363" data-end="393">
<p data-start="365" data-end="393">“Your repositories” me jao</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1ru8zz3" data-start="394" data-end="458">
<p data-start="396" data-end="458"><strong data-start="396" data-end="431">Apni repo ke NAME pe click karo</strong> (e.g. <code data-start="438" data-end="455">video-generator</code>)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="460" data-end="536">⚠️ Jab tak aap repo ke andar nahi jaoge, <strong data-start="501" data-end="534">Settings / Pages nahi dikhega</strong></p>
<hr data-start="538" data-end="541">
<h1 data-section-id="1y6j4bb" data-start="543" data-end="578"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="547" data-end="578">Step 2: Settings tab dhundo</strong></span></h1>
<p data-start="579" data-end="624">Repo open hone ke baad upar ye tabs dikhenge:</p>
<ul data-start="626" data-end="727">
<li data-section-id="1uweazp" data-start="626" data-end="634">
<p data-start="628" data-end="634">Code</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="sztk2" data-start="635" data-end="645">
<p data-start="637" data-end="645">Issues</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="518brj" data-start="646" data-end="663">
<p data-start="648" data-end="663">Pull requests</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1oieezp" data-start="664" data-end="675">
<p data-start="666" data-end="675">Actions</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1hrhwwe" data-start="676" data-end="688">
<p data-start="678" data-end="688">Projects</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1ghiddd" data-start="689" data-end="727">
<p data-start="691" data-end="727"><strong data-start="691" data-end="706">Settings ⚙️</strong> ← ye important hai</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="729" data-end="758">👉 <strong data-start="732" data-end="758">Settings pe click karo</strong></p>
<hr data-start="760" data-end="763">
<h1 data-section-id="1om5hhj" data-start="765" data-end="800"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="769" data-end="800">Step 3: Pages option dhundo</strong></span></h1>
<p data-start="801" data-end="819">Settings ke andar:</p>
<p data-start="821" data-end="878">👉 Left side me scroll karo<br data-start="848" data-end="851">
👉 Niche milega <strong data-start="867" data-end="878">“Pages”</strong></p>
<p data-start="880" data-end="937">⚠️ Kabhi kabhi thoda niche hota hai, scroll zaroor karo</p>
<hr data-start="939" data-end="942">
<h1 data-section-id="1wv2u7t" data-start="944" data-end="983">❗ Agar “Pages” phir bhi nahi mil raha</h1>
<h2 data-section-id="18kk37i" data-start="985" data-end="1015">🔴 Reason 1: Repo empty hai</h2>
<p data-start="1016" data-end="1034">👉 Ensure karo ke:</p>
<ul data-start="1035" data-end="1098">
<li data-section-id="18erwt6" data-start="1035" data-end="1070">
<p data-start="1037" data-end="1070"><code data-start="1037" data-end="1049">index.html</code> upload ho chuki ho</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1v3wl6v" data-start="1071" data-end="1098">
<p data-start="1073" data-end="1098">File repo me visible ho</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1100" data-end="1103">

<p data-start="1140" data-end="1166">👉 Aap yahan hone chahiye:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1167" data-end="1212"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="w-full overflow-x-hidden overflow-y-auto pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none; max-height: 433px;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>https://github.com/USERNAME/REPO_NAME</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<h1 data-section-id="19zpi1b" data-start="254" data-end="296"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="258" data-end="296">Ab ye step follow karo (IMPORTANT)</strong></span></h1>
<h2 data-section-id="vexiiq" data-start="298" data-end="340"><span role="text">🔽 <strong data-start="304" data-end="340">Step 1: Left side ko scroll karo</strong></span></h2>

<p data-start="366" data-end="451">👉 Left sidebar me dhyan se dekho<br data-start="399" data-end="402">
👉 Aur <strong data-start="409" data-end="449">NEECHE scroll karo (bahut niche tak)</strong></p>

<ul data-start="473" data-end="558">

👉 Aur unke niche <strong data-start="545" data-end="556">“Pages”</strong></p>
</li>

<p data-start="661" data-end="701">Settings page ke top pe search hota hai:</p>
<p data-start="703" data-end="730">👉 Wahan likho: <strong data-start="719" data-end="728">Pages</strong></p>

<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="850" data-end="927"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="w-full overflow-x-hidden overflow-y-auto pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none; max-height: 433px;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/YOUR_REPO/settings/pages</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<hr data-start="963" data-end="966">
<h1 data-section-id="1kzcfzu" data-start="968" data-end="1012">❗ Agar phir bhi nahi mil raha (REAL ISSUE)</h1>
<h3 data-section-id="laccxm" data-start="1014" data-end="1055">🔴 Case 1: Repo abhi bilkul empty hai</h3>
<p data-start="1056" data-end="1070">👉 Check karo:</p>
<ul data-start="1071" data-end="1152">
<li data-section-id="1cpshvc" data-start="1071" data-end="1112">
<p data-start="1073" data-end="1112">Kya <code data-start="1077" data-end="1089">index.html</code> file upload hui hai?</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="g4l903" data-start="1113" data-end="1152">
<p data-start="1115" data-end="1152">Kya wo “Code” tab me dikh rahi hai?</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1154" data-end="1167">👉 Agar nahi:</p>
<ul data-start="1168" data-end="1216">
<li data-section-id="laohim" data-start="1168" data-end="1194">
<p data-start="1170" data-end="1194">Pehle file upload karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="gl5psx" data-start="1195" data-end="1216">
<p data-start="1197" data-end="1216">Phir refresh karo</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1218" data-end="1221">
<h3 data-section-id="cwixlk" data-start="1223" data-end="1257">🔴 Case 2: Aap wrong tab me ho</h3>
<p data-start="1258" data-end="1278">👉 Confirm karo aap:</p>
<ul data-start="1279" data-end="1343">
<li data-section-id="1ge3z0w" data-start="1279" data-end="1313">
<p data-start="1281" data-end="1313"><strong data-start="1281" data-end="1305">Settings (repo wala)</strong> me ho</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1k67rd1" data-start="1314" data-end="1343">
<p data-start="1316" data-end="1343">Na ke account settings me</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1345" data-end="1348">
<h3 data-section-id="nrvz4x" data-start="1350" data-end="1381">🔴 Case 3: Screen small hai</h3>

<h1 data-section-id="4fkxn8" data-start="216" data-end="248"><span role="text"><strong data-start="218" data-end="248">Step 1: Branch select karo</strong></span></h1>
<ol data-start="250" data-end="289">
<li data-section-id="o7s753" data-start="250" data-end="289">
<p data-start="253" data-end="289">Pages section me ek option milega:</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="291" data-end="338"><strong data-start="291" data-end="303">“Source”</strong> → yahan branch select karna hai.</p>
<ul data-start="340" data-end="491">
<li data-section-id="1klhltk" data-start="340" data-end="415">
<p data-start="342" data-end="415">Dropdown me <strong data-start="354" data-end="362">main</strong> select karo (agar aapki file <code data-start="392" data-end="398">main</code> branch me hai)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="to3h76" data-start="416" data-end="491">
<p data-start="418" data-end="491">Folder = <code data-start="427" data-end="437">/ (root)</code> choose karo (kyunki aapka <code data-start="464" data-end="476">index.html</code> root me hai)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<blockquote data-start="493" data-end="623">
<p data-start="495" data-end="623">Ye kaam karega ke GitHub ko pata chal jaaye:<br data-start="539" data-end="542">
“Is branch ke root folder me jo <code data-start="576" data-end="588">index.html</code> hai, wo website ka homepage hoga.”</p>
</blockquote>

<hr data-start="117" data-end="120">
<h1 data-section-id="okeg2h" data-start="122" data-end="160"><span role="text"><strong data-start="124" data-end="160">1️⃣ GitHub Username change karna</strong></span></h1>
<p data-start="162" data-end="252">Aapka username (<code data-start="178" data-end="186">zahi33</code>) ko change karke <code data-start="204" data-end="217">ZaheerAbbas</code> karna possible hai, steps ye hain:</p>
<ol data-start="254" data-end="472">
<li data-section-id="fa0uia" data-start="254" data-end="315">
<p data-start="257" data-end="315">GitHub open karo → Top right profile icon → <strong data-start="301" data-end="313">Settings</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="kp6tkh" data-start="316" data-end="348">
<p data-start="319" data-end="348"><strong data-start="319" data-end="339">Account settings</strong> me jao</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1g5oon6" data-start="349" data-end="388">
<p data-start="352" data-end="388"><strong data-start="352" data-end="371">Change username</strong> option dhoondo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="dzvhvu" data-start="389" data-end="452">
<p data-start="392" data-end="452">Naya username type karo → GitHub check karega availability</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="z7aain" data-start="453" data-end="472">
<p data-start="456" data-end="472">Confirm → Save</p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote data-start="474" data-end="712">
<p data-start="476" data-end="489">⚠️ Warning:</p>
<ul data-start="492" data-end="712">
<li data-section-id="14pb1dq" data-start="492" data-end="607">
<p data-start="494" data-end="607">Agar aap username change karte ho, purani repo links (<a data-start="548" data-end="575" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="decorated-link cursor-pointer">https://github.com/zahi33/…<span aria-hidden="true" class="ms-0.5 inline-block align-middle leading-none"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" data-rtl-flip="" class="block h-[0.75em] w-[0.75em] stroke-current stroke-[0.75]"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#304883" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></span></a>) ka link <strong data-start="585" data-end="604">break ho jayega</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="2fmcjm" data-start="610" data-end="712">
<p data-start="612" data-end="712">GitHub automatically redirect ka option deta hai, lekin sometimes kuch links broken ho sakte hain.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
<hr data-start="714" data-end="717">
<h1 data-section-id="1xfxhl6" data-start="719" data-end="765"><span role="text"><strong data-start="721" data-end="765">2️⃣ Repository / GitHub Pages URL update</strong></span></h1>
<p data-start="767" data-end="806">Agar aap username change kar dete ho:</p>
<ul data-start="808" data-end="849">
<li data-section-id="pjexrk" data-start="808" data-end="849">
<p data-start="810" data-end="849">Aapki Pages URL bhi change ho jayegi:</p>
</li>
</ul>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="851" data-end="957"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="w-full overflow-x-hidden overflow-y-auto pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none; max-height: 433px;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>Old: https://zahi33.github.io/video-generator/</span><br><span>New: https://ZaheerAbbas.github.io/video-generator/</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<hr data-start="1030" data-end="1033">
<h1 data-section-id="1bb4c8g" data-start="1035" data-end="1059"><span role="text"><strong data-start="1037" data-end="1059">3️⃣ Recommendation</strong></span></h1>
<ul data-start="1061" data-end="1280">
<li data-section-id="yn1r4n" data-start="1061" data-end="1167">
<p data-start="1063" data-end="1167">Agar abhi live karne se pehle username change karna hai → Pehle change karo, phir <strong data-start="1145" data-end="1165">Pages setup karo</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="mqk0i6" data-start="1168" data-end="1280">
<p data-start="1170" data-end="1280">Agar site already live kar chuke ho → Username change karna slightly risky ho sakta hai (redirects ka issue)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1282" data-end="1285">
<p data-start="1287" data-end="1300">💡 <strong data-start="1290" data-end="1298">Tip:</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1301" data-end="1420">
<li data-section-id="1ef3uoq" data-start="1301" data-end="1375">
<p data-start="1303" data-end="1375">Username change ke baad repo name aur Pages settings <strong data-start="1356" data-end="1373">recheck karna</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="n4bat9" data-start="1376" data-end="1420">
<p data-start="1378" data-end="1420"><code data-start="1378" data-end="1390">index.html</code> root me ho → site live rahe</p>
</li>
</ul>

<p data-start="1427" data-end="1568">Agar chaho, main <strong data-start="1444" data-end="1476">step-by-step guide bana doon</strong>:<br data-start="1477" data-end="1480">
<strong data-start="1480" data-end="1538">Username change → repo check → GitHub Pages live setup</strong> taake koi link break na ho.</p>

<hr data-start="175" data-end="178">
<h2 data-section-id="1ll557j" data-start="180" data-end="219"><span role="text"><strong data-start="183" data-end="219">1️⃣ Branch ya repo name mismatch</strong></span></h2>
<ul data-start="221" data-end="247">
<li data-section-id="1wndb19" data-start="221" data-end="247">
<p data-start="223" data-end="247">Screenshot me URL hai:</p>
</li>

<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="248" data-end="329"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="w-full overflow-x-hidden overflow-y-auto pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none; max-height: 433px;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>https://github.com/zaheerabbashacks/Video-Generator/settings/pages/source</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>
<ul data-start="330" data-end="490">
<li data-section-id="vr6c0r" data-start="330" data-end="490">
<p data-start="332" data-end="345">Check karo:</p>
<ul data-start="348" data-end="490">
<li data-section-id="ahbt05" data-start="348" data-end="427">
<p data-start="350" data-end="427">Repo name exact <code data-start="366" data-end="383">Video-Generator</code> hai ya lowercase/uppercase me difference?</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="hphibx" data-start="430" data-end="490">
<p data-start="432" data-end="490">Username exact <code data-start="447" data-end="465">zaheerabbashacks</code> hai ya change ho gaya?</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<blockquote data-start="492" data-end="582">
<p data-start="494" data-end="582">GitHub is case-sensitive hai URLs me. Agar ek letter bhi mismatch hua → 404 aa jata hai.</p>
</blockquote>
<hr data-start="584" data-end="587">
<h2 data-section-id="1c3yeec" data-start="589" data-end="650"><span role="text"><strong data-start="592" data-end="650">2️⃣ Page ke liye “Source” branch properly set nahi hai</strong></span></h2>
<ul data-start="652" data-end="757">
<li data-section-id="1f33dyc" data-start="652" data-end="706">
<p data-start="654" data-end="706">Pages tab me branch select karni hoti hai (<code data-start="697" data-end="703">main</code>)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="f5b677" data-start="707" data-end="757">
<p data-start="709" data-end="757">Agar branch empty hai → GitHub 404 show karega</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="759" data-end="762">
<h2 data-section-id="1tevm5u" data-start="764" data-end="784"><span role="text"><strong data-start="767" data-end="784">3️⃣ Wrong URL</strong></span></h2>
<ul data-start="786" data-end="940">
<li data-section-id="cakb2j" data-start="786" data-end="876">
<p data-start="788" data-end="876">Jo aap open kar rahe ho wo <strong data-start="815" data-end="848">source page ka direct URL hai</strong> (<code data-start="850" data-end="873">settings/pages/source</code>)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="10kcdcm" data-start="877" data-end="940">
<p data-start="879" data-end="940">Normal live site check karne ke liye ye open karna chahiye:</p>
</li>
</ul>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="941" data-end="986"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="w-full overflow-x-hidden overflow-y-auto pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none; max-height: 433px;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>https://USERNAME.github.io/REPO_NAME/</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<p data-start="1063" data-end="1154">Settings ka URL <strong data-start="1079" data-end="1113">directly live website nahi hai</strong>, ye sirf Pages setup ke liye hota hai.</p>
</blockquote>
<hr data-start="1156" data-end="1159">
<h3 data-section-id="h2vsez" data-start="1161" data-end="1185"><span role="text">✅ <strong data-start="1167" data-end="1185">Solution Steps</strong></span></h3>
<ol data-start="1187" data-end="1450">
<li data-section-id="zagyck" data-start="1187" data-end="1243">
<p data-start="1190" data-end="1243">Apni repository open karo (repo ke andar, code tab)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1dtp8k2" data-start="1244" data-end="1314">
<p data-start="1247" data-end="1314">Settings → Pages → Source → Branch <code data-start="1282" data-end="1288">main</code> → Folder <code data-start="1298" data-end="1305">/root</code> → Save</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="rdld76" data-start="1315" data-end="1349">
<p data-start="1318" data-end="1349">Thodi der wait karo (1–2 min)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="me2o64" data-start="1350" data-end="1450">
<p data-start="1353" data-end="1450">Wahan jo <strong data-start="1362" data-end="1382">GitHub Pages URL</strong> show ho raha hai → usko open karo (na ki <code data-start="1424" data-end="1447">settings/pages/source</code>)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote data-start="1452" data-end="1464">
<p data-start="1454" data-end="1464">Example:</p>
</blockquote>

<h1 data-section-id="1p6ffd8" data-start="192" data-end="244"><span role="text"><strong data-start="194" data-end="244">GitHub Pages Live Website Setup – Zaheer Style</strong></span></h1>
<hr data-start="246" data-end="249">
<h2 data-section-id="nfsmnx" data-start="251" data-end="286"><span role="text"><strong data-start="254" data-end="286">Step 1: Repository open karo</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="287" data-end="465">
<li data-section-id="1tae977" data-start="287" data-end="327">
<p data-start="290" data-end="327">Browser me jao → <a data-start="307" data-end="325" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="decorated-link" href="https://github.com/">https://github.com<span aria-hidden="true" class="ms-0.5 inline-block align-middle leading-none"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" data-rtl-flip="" class="block h-[0.75em] w-[0.75em] stroke-current stroke-[0.75]"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#304883" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></span></a></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1udd4bx" data-start="328" data-end="343">
<p data-start="331" data-end="343">Login karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="hg1htk" data-start="344" data-end="409">
<p data-start="347" data-end="409">Top right profile icon → <strong data-start="372" data-end="393">Your repositories</strong> pe click karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1kwi742" data-start="410" data-end="465">
<p data-start="413" data-end="465">Apni repo select karo (example: <code data-start="445" data-end="462">Video-Generator</code>)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="467" data-end="504">✅ Ab aap repo ke <strong data-start="484" data-end="496">Code tab</strong> me ho</p>
<hr data-start="506" data-end="509">
<h2 data-section-id="1g4s61r" data-start="511" data-end="536"><span role="text"><strong data-start="514" data-end="536">Step 2: Check file</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="537" data-end="658">
<li data-section-id="1mj7k01" data-start="537" data-end="593">
<p data-start="540" data-end="593">Code tab me ensure karo <strong data-start="564" data-end="580"><code data-start="566" data-end="578">index.html</code></strong> visible ho</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="11stsms" data-start="594" data-end="658">
<p data-start="597" data-end="658">Ye file root folder me honi chahiye (koi subfolder me nahi)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="660" data-end="701"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="w-full overflow-x-hidden overflow-y-auto pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none; max-height: 433px;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>Repo/</span><br><span> └── index.html   ← correct</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="703" data-end="706">
<h2 data-section-id="8q0mrc" data-start="708" data-end="741"><span role="text"><strong data-start="711" data-end="741">Step 3: Settings open karo</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="742" data-end="850">
<li data-section-id="160p84j" data-start="742" data-end="795">
<p data-start="745" data-end="795">Repo ke top tabs me → <strong data-start="767" data-end="782">Settings ⚙️</strong> click karo</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="5yy9h" data-start="796" data-end="850">
<p data-start="799" data-end="850">Left sidebar me scroll → <strong data-start="824" data-end="833">Pages</strong> option dhoondo</p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote data-start="852" data-end="940">
<p data-start="854" data-end="940">Agar Pages dikh nahi raha → left side scroll karo ya search bar me “Pages” type karo</p>
</blockquote>
<hr data-start="942" data-end="945">
<h2 data-section-id="q4801n" data-start="947" data-end="980"><span role="text"><strong data-start="950" data-end="980">Step 4: GitHub Pages setup</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="981" data-end="1078">
<li data-section-id="u1rzfh" data-start="981" data-end="1058">
<p data-start="984" data-end="1008"><strong data-start="984" data-end="994">Source</strong> section me:</p>
<ul data-start="1012" data-end="1058">
<li data-section-id="suj222" data-start="1012" data-end="1031">
<p data-start="1014" data-end="1031">Branch = <code data-start="1023" data-end="1029">main</code></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="oowc17" data-start="1035" data-end="1058">
<p data-start="1037" data-end="1058">Folder = <code data-start="1046" data-end="1056">/ (root)</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1ph4tw6" data-start="1059" data-end="1078">
<p data-start="1062" data-end="1078">Click <strong data-start="1068" data-end="1076">Save</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote data-start="1080" data-end="1161">
<p data-start="1082" data-end="1161">GitHub thoda time lega (1–2 min)<br data-start="1114" data-end="1117">
Successful setup ke baad message aayega:</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1162" data-end="1259"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-lbtco6v1.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="w-full overflow-x-hidden overflow-y-auto pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none; max-height: 433px;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>Your site is ready to be published at https://zaheerabbashacks.github.io/Video-Generator/</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<h2 data-section-id="1fejewx" data-start="1266" data-end="1298"><span role="text"><strong data-start="1269" data-end="1298">Step 5: Open live website</strong></span></h2>
<ol data-start="1299" data-end="1529">
<li data-section-id="1r71io0" data-start="1299" data-end="1333">
<p data-start="1302" data-end="1333">Jo URL upar mila → click karo</p>

<li data-section-id="1k7ir1b" data-start="1334" data-end="1402">
<p data-start="1337" data-end="1402">Browser me aapka <strong data-start="1354" data-end="1390">single-page dark video generator</strong> show hoga</p>

</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>

<h2 data-section-id="144rqfw" data-start="1536" data-end="1561"><span role="text"><strong data-start="1539" data-end="1561">Step 6: Test video</strong></span></h2>
